## Idea

The standard finite types are defined inductively by `Fin 0 := empty` and
`Fin (n+1) := (Fin n) + 1`. **Note** that the outermost coproduct (i.e. the
`inr` injection) is the _top_ element, when `Fin n` is considered as an initial
segment of `ℕ`.

## Definition

### The standard finite types in universe level zero

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-Setᵉ"></a><a id="1972" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">Fin-Setᵉ</a> <a id="1981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1983" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a> <a id="1986" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1988" href="foundation-core.sets%25E1%25B5%2589.html#897" class="Function">Setᵉ</a> <a id="1993" href="Agda.Primitive.html#915" class="Primitive">lzero</a>

<a id="2029" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">Fin-Setᵉ</a> <a id="2038" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2039" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="2047" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2047" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="2049" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2051" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2053" href="foundation.equality-coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13252" class="Function">coproduct-Setᵉ</a> <a id="2068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2069" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1972" class="Function">Fin-Setᵉ</a> <a id="2078" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2047" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="2080" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2082" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3309" class="Function">unit-Setᵉ</a>

<a id="3383" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3296" class="Function">neq-inl-Fin-inr-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3404" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3405" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="3413" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3413" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="3415" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3418" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="3423" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3423" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="3425" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3427" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="3431" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3296" class="Function">neq-inl-Fin-inr-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3452" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3413" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="3455" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3423" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="3458" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="3461" href="foundation.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2792" class="Function">is-injective-inlᵉ</a>
<a id="3479" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3296" class="Function">neq-inl-Fin-inr-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3501" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="3509" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3509" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="3511" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3514" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="3519" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="3524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3526" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3528" href="foundation.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2976" class="Function">neq-inl-inrᵉ</a>

<a id="neq-inr-Fin-inl-Finᵉ"></a><a id="3542" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3542" class="Function">neq-inr-Fin-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3563" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="3567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3568" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3568" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="3571" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3573" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="3575" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3580" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3580" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="3583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3585" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="3590" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3568" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="3592" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3594" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3596" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3140" class="Function">inr-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3605" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3568" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="3608" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3580" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="3611" href="foundation.negated-equality%25E1%25B5%2589.html#760" class="Function Operator">≠ᵉ</a> <a id="3614" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2243" class="Function">inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3623" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3568" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="3626" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3580" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="3629" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3542" class="Function">neq-inr-Fin-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3651" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="3659" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3659" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="3661" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3664" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="3669" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3669" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="3671" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3673" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="3677" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3542" class="Function">neq-inr-Fin-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="3698" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3659" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="3701" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3669" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="3704" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="3707" href="foundation.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2792" class="Function">is-injective-inlᵉ</a>

## Properties

### Being on the left is decidable

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-decidable-is-inl-Finᵉ"></a><a id="4337" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4337" class="Function">is-decidable-is-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="4362" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="4366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4367" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4367" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="4370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4372" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="4374" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4377" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4377" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="4380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4382" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="4387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4388" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="4396" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4367" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="4398" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4403" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1541" class="Function">is-decidableᵉ</a> <a id="4417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4418" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2771" class="Function">is-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="4430" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4367" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="4433" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4377" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="4435" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4437" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4337" class="Function">is-decidable-is-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="4462" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4462" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="4465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4466" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="4471" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4471" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="4473" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4475" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4477" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="4482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4483" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4471" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="4486" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="4489" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a><a id="4494" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4496" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4337" class="Function">is-decidable-is-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="4521" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4521" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="4524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4525" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="4530" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="4535" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4537" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4539" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="4544" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4557" class="Function">αᵉ</a>
  <a id="4549" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="4557" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4557" class="Function">αᵉ</a> <a id="4560" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4562" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2771" class="Function">is-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="4574" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4521" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="4577" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4578" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="4583" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="4588" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4590" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4592" href="foundation-core.empty-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#811" class="Datatype">emptyᵉ</a>
  <a id="4601" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4557" class="Function">αᵉ</a> <a id="4604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4605" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4605" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="4608" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="4611" class="Symbol">())</a>
</pre>

### The zero elements in the standard finite types

<pre class="Agda"><a id="zero-Finᵉ"></a><a id="6036" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="6046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6049" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6049" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="6052" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6054" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="6056" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6058" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6060" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="6065" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6066" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="6074" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6049" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="6076" class="Symbol">)</a>

<pre class="Agda"><a id="bounded-succ-Finᵉ"></a><a id="7117" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7117" class="Function">bounded-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="7135" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7138" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7138" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7143" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7147" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7149" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="7154" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7138" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7157" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7159" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="7164" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7138" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="7167" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7117" class="Function">bounded-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="7185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7186" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7194" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7194" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="7196" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7199" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="7204" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7204" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="7206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7208" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7210" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6541" class="Function">skip-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="7225" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7194" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7228" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7204" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="7231" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7117" class="Function">bounded-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="7249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7250" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="7258" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7258" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="7260" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7262" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7263" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="7268" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="7273" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7275" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7277" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="7282" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a>
</pre>
### The inclusion of `Fin k` into `ℕ`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="nat-Finᵉ"></a><a id="7340" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="7349" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7352" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7352" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7355" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7357" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7359" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7361" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7363" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="7368" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7352" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7373" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a>

<a id="nat-Fin-reverseᵉ"></a><a id="7463" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7463" class="Function">nat-Fin-reverseᵉ</a> <a id="7480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7483" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7483" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7486" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7488" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="7490" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7494" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="7499" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7483" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="7502" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7504" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a>

    <a id="7801" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7803" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7740" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="7805" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="8157" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7728" class="Function">preserves-leq-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8179" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8180" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="8189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8190" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="8198" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8139" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="8200" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8202" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8149" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="8204" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8206" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8139" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8210" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7960" class="Function">upper-bound-nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="8231" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8139" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="8234" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8149" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="8236" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="9201" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="9206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9207" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9123" class="Function">emb-nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="9220" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9220" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="9222" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9224" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9226" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8991" class="Function">is-emb-nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="9242" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9220" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
</pre>
### The retraction of `ℕ` into `Fin k`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-natᵉ"></a><a id="9298" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9298" class="Function">Fin-natᵉ</a> <a id="9307" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9310" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="9313" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9315" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="9317" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9319" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9321" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a> <a id="9324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9326" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="9331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9332" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="9340" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="9342" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Exercise 7.5 (c)

<pre class="Agda"><a id="neq-zero-skip-zero-Finᵉ"></a><a id="11196" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11196" class="Function">neq-zero-skip-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11220" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="11224" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11225" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11225" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11228" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11230" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="11232" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11235" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11235" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="11238" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11240" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="11245" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11225" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11247" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11249" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="11253" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6353" class="Function">is-nonzero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11269" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11270" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11278" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11225" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11280" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11283" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6541" class="Function">skip-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11298" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11225" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="11301" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11235" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11303" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11305" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11196" class="Function">neq-zero-skip-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11329" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11330" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11338" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11338" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11340" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11343" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="11348" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11348" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11350" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11352" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11352" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="11355" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="11359" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11196" class="Function">neq-zero-skip-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11383" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11384" class="Argument">kᵉ</a> <a id="11387" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11389" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11338" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11391" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11393" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11394" class="Argument">xᵉ</a> <a id="11397" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11399" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11348" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="11401" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11403" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11404" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11058" class="Function">is-injective-inl-Finᵉ</a> <a id="11426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11427" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="11435" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11338" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="11437" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11439" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11352" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="11441" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="12515" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12197" class="Function">is-injective-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12539" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12547" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12547" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12549" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12552" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="12557" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="12562" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12564" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12565" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12570" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12570" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="12572" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12574" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12574" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="12577" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12581" href="foundation-core.empty-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#927" class="Function">ex-falsoᵉ</a> <a id="12591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12592" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11444" class="Function">neq-zero-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12612" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12620" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12547" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12624" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12625" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12630" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12570" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="12632" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12634" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12635" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="12639" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12644" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12645" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="12650" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12574" class="Bound">pᵉ</a><a id="12652" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="12656" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12197" class="Function">is-injective-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12679" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12680" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12688" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12688" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12690" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12693" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="12698" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="12703" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12705" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12706" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="12711" href="foundation.unit-type%25E1%25B5%2589.html#873" class="InductiveConstructor">starᵉ</a><a id="12716" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12718" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12718" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="12721" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12723" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a>
</pre>
We define a function `skip-neg-two-Fin` in order to define `pred-Fin`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="skip-neg-two-Finᵉ"></a><a id="12814" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12832" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12837" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12837" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12842" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="12844" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12846" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12848" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="12853" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12837" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="12856" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12858" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="12863" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12864" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12872" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12837" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12874" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12876" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12895" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12903" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12903" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12908" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12913" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12913" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12917" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12919" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12924" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12925" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="12930" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12913" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12932" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12934" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12953" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12961" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12961" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="12963" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12966" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="12971" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12971" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="12973" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12975" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12977" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="12990" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12991" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="12999" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12961" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13001" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We define the predecessor function on `Fin k`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="pred-Finᵉ"></a><a id="13064" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13074" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13076" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13077" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13077" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13080" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13082" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="13084" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13086" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13088" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="13093" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13077" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13096" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13098" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="13103" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13077" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="13106" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13116" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13117" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13125" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13125" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13127" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13129" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13130" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="13135" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13135" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="13137" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13139" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13141" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13159" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13125" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13162" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13163" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13173" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13125" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13176" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13135" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="13178" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13180" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13190" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13191" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13199" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13199" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13201" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13204" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#496" class="InductiveConstructor">inrᵉ</a> <a id="13209" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13209" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="13211" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13213" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13215" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2645" class="Function">neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13228" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13199" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
</pre>
We now turn to the exercise.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="pred-zero-Finᵉ"></a><a id="13274" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13274" class="Function">pred-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13289" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13293" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13294" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13294" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13297" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13299" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="13301" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13305" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2538" class="Function">is-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13321" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13322" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13330" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13294" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13332" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13334" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13335" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13346" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13354" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13294" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13356" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13359" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13369" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13294" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13371" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="13374" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13274" class="Function">pred-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13390" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a><a id="13397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13399" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13401" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a>
<a id="13407" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13274" class="Function">pred-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13423" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13431" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13431" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13435" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13437" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="13441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13442" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13461" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13469" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13431" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13471" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13475" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13274" class="Function">pred-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13490" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13431" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13492" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="succ-skip-neg-two-Finᵉ"></a><a id="13495" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13495" class="Function">succ-skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13518" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13523" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13523" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="13526" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13528" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="13530" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13533" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13533" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="13536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13538" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="13543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13544" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13552" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13523" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13554" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13557" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="13561" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6721" class="Function">succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13572" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13581" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13589" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13523" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13591" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13595" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12814" class="Function">skip-neg-two-Finᵉ</a> <a id="13613" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13614" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="13622" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13523" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="13624" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13626" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13533" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="13628" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13630" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a>

### `Fin` is a preunivalent type family

The proof does not rely on the (pre-)univalence axiom.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-section-on-diagonal-is-equivalence-injective-Finᵉ"></a><a id="17261" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17261" class="Function">is-section-on-diagonal-is-equivalence-injective-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17314" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="17318" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17319" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17319" class="Bound">nᵉ</a> <a id="17322" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17324" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="17326" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17328" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="17332" href="foundation.transport-along-identifications%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1592" class="Function">equiv-trᵉ</a> <a id="17342" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="17347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17348" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16133" class="Function">is-equivalence-injective-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17379" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17319" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17381" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17383" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17384" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17319" class="Bound">nᵉ</a><a id="17386" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17388" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4139" class="Function">id-equivᵉ</a><a id="17397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17399" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="17402" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4139" class="Function">id-equivᵉ</a>
<a id="17412" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17261" class="Function">is-section-on-diagonal-is-equivalence-injective-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17465" class="Symbol">=</a>
